for (int i = 0; i < nums.length; i++){
    for (int j = i+1; j < nums.length; j++){
        if (nums[i]+ nums[j] == target){
                return new int[] {i. j}
            }
    }
}

def twoSum(nums, target):
    p, q = 0, len(nums) - 1

    while p < q:
        v = nums[p] + nums[q]
        if v == traget:
            return p + 1, q+1
        
        # update pointer
        if v < target:
            p += 1
        else:
            q -= 1 ^PoK9SlbK

def sol (s):
 window = set()
l = 0
res = 0

for i in range(lenght(s):
    # first remove it
    while s[i] in window:
        window.remove(s[l]
         l += 1

    window.add(s[i])
    res = max (res, i - l + 1)

return res ^ZtOV6VJZ

s, l, ans = 0, 0, 0
for i, val in enumerate(nums):
    s += val
    while s >= target:
        ans = min(ans, i - l + 1)
        s -= nums[l]
        l += 1
 ^qRuKLj1j
